ANNEX   I  Schedule of Brunei Darussalam  Headnote  Elimination of Customs Duties on Goods Originating in Chile, New Zealand or Singapore     Introductory notes  I. The tariff schedule in this Annex contains the following four columns:  (a) “Code”: the code used in the nomenclature of the ASEAN Harmonised Tariff Nomenclature  (AHTN) 2004.  (b) “Description”: the description of the product falling under the heading.  (c) “Base Rate”: the basic customs duty from which the tariff elimination programme starts.  (d) “End date”: the year in which the tariff goes to zero (i.e. tariff free) for the product concerned.   II. Except as otherwise provided in this Agreement, Brunei Darussalam shall progressively eliminate its customs duties on originating goods of Chile, New Zealand and Singapore in accordance with its Tariff Schedule in this Annex.  The base rate and the interim rate of customs duty at each stage of reduction for an item are indicated for the item in the Schedule.  Reductions shall occur on 1 January of each year, as provided for in the Schedule.
